   function loadCSS( href, before, media ){
  "use strict";
  // Arguments explained:
  // `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
  // `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our &lt;link&gt;
  // By default, `before` uses the first &lt;script&gt; element in the page.
  // However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
  // If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
  // note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
  var ss = window.document.createElement( "link" );
  var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName( "script" )[ 0 ];
  var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
  ss.rel = "stylesheet";
  ss.href = href;
  // temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
  ss.media = "only x";
  // inject link
  ref.parentNode.insertBefore( ss, ref );
  // This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
  // It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
  function toggleMedia(){
    var defined;
    for( var i = 0; i &lt; sheets.length; i++ ){
      if( sheets[ i ].href &amp;&amp; sheets[ i ].href.indexOf( href ) &gt; -1 ){
        defined = true;
      }
    }
    if( defined ){
      ss.media = media || "all";
    }
    else {
      setTimeout( toggleMedia );
    }

         </path>
        </g>
       </svg>
      </div>
      <a class="l-h-home icon-button" href="/">
       <svg version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 342 71" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink">

      <div class="p-a-header">
       <h1 class="p-a-title" itemprop="headline">
        This R-Rated Power Rangers Short Film is Violent, Bloody, and Straight Up BADASS!
       </h1>
       <div class="p-a-meta">
        by
        <a class="p-a-author" data-track="navigate:public-profile:article-desc" href="/timgonzales" itemprop="author">
         Tim Gonzales
        </a>
        
        <span class="p-a-timestamp">
         Posted on
         <meta content="2015-02-24T09:31:41-08:00" itemprop="datePublished"/>
         <meta content="2015-02-27T20:54:02-08:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
         <time class="la_time" data-date-format="normal" datetime="2015-02-24T17:31:41.000Z">
          February 24th, 2015 at 10:31am
         </time>
        </span>
        <small class="p-a-edited">
          Last edit on
         <time class="la_time" data-date-format="short" datetime="2015-02-28T04:54:02.000Z">
          February 27th, 2015
         </time>
        </small>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="p-a-content pure-g">
       <figure class="p-a-cover pure-u-1 pure-u-lg-16-24">
        <div class="p-a-c-imgwrap">
         <img alt="Art by Dave Rapoza" itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_480,w_640/t_mp_quality/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-91280b9d-1039-4411-a6ba-d57c0898da45-png-275659.jpg" title="Art by Dave Rapoza"/>
        </div>
        <figcaption>
         Art by Dave Rapoza
        </figcaption>
       </figure>
       <aside class="p-a-sidebar pure-u-1 pure-u-lg-8-24">
        <section class="p-a-authorcard" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
         <div class="p-a-ac-content pure-g">
          <a class="p-a-ac-imgwrap pure-u-1-3" data-track="navigate:public-profile:article-sidebar" href="/timgonzales" itemprop="url">
           <img alt="Tim Gonzales" itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_100,t_mp_quality,w_100/tim-gonzales-1c12dd65-a8b5-47da-8cfa-548c7376a0ab.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <div class="p-a-ac-body pure-u-2-3">
           <a class="p-a-ac-authorname" data-track="navigate:public-profile:article-sidebar" href="/timgonzales" itemprop="name">
            Tim Gonzales
           </a>
           <small itemprop="description">
            I burn toast and hardly sleep. My favorite food is champorado. Follow me on twitter! @timgonzales
           </small>
           <div class="p-a-ac-follow">
            <div class="m-follow" data-context="post-sidebar" data-follow="user:1016822">

        <div class="b-sticky_sidebar">
         <div class="m-gad m-gad-sidebar_ad">
         </div>
         <span class="b-ss-share" data-type="facebook">

       <div class="m-gad m-gad-mid_ad">
       </div>
       <div class="p-a-body pure-u-1 pure-u-lg-16-24" itemprop="articleBody">
        <article class="p-a-text">
         <h3>
          Lionsgate had better be worried about their upcoming
          <i>
           Power Rangers
          </i>
          movie.
          <br/>
         </h3>
         <figure data-id="275736">
          <video autoplay="autoplay" loop="loop" muted="muted" poster="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.jpg">
           <source src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.mp4" type="video/mp4">
           </source>
           <source src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.webm" type="video/webm">
           </source>
           <div class="mx-gif" data-pause_src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.jpg" data-play_src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.gif">
            <img src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.jpg"/>
            <i class="icon-play">
            </i>
            <div class="m-spinner">
             <i class="icon-spin">
             </i>
            </div>
           </div>
          </video>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Why? Because film producer Adi Shankarthe man responsible for such awesome comic book related shorts as
          <i>
           <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7YDYL6oECjU" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
            Venom: Truth in Journalism
           </a>
          </i>
          and
          <i>
           <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bWpK0wsnitc" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
            The Punisher: Dirty Laundry
           </a>
          </i>
          just slapped the internet across the face with a big bag full of awesome bricks in the form of a
          <i>
           <a href="http://moviepilot.com/tags/power-rangers">
            Power Rangers
           </a>
          </i>
          short film put together by renowned music video director Joseph Kahn.
         </p>
         <p>
          <b>
           This gritty take on a beloved franchise kicks so much ass, and it's righteously nuts. *NSFW* Prepare to have your mind blown:
          </b>
         </p>
         <p>
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" class="embedly-embed" frameborder="0" height="366" scrolling="no" src="//cdn.embedly.com/widgets/media.html?src=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fembed%2Fvw5vcUPyL90%3Ffeature%3Doembed&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3Dvw5vcUPyL90&amp;image=http%3A%2F%2Fi.ytimg.com%2Fvi%2Fvw5vcUPyL90%2Fhqdefault.jpg&amp;key=4346f5e0fac645ec8a30f75e92dc526f&amp;type=text%2Fhtml&amp;schema=youtube" width="650">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          Sci-fi veteran Katee Sackhoff (
          <i>
           Battlestar Galactica, Riddick
          </i>
          ) as The Pink Ranger/Kimberly? Pretty awesome. James Van Der Beek (
          <i>
           Dawson's Creek
          </i>
          ) hamming it up as the primary antagonist and ex-Red Ranger Rocky? Also awesome. These are two actors with fairly decent fanbases who I would never have expected to show up in any kind of
          <i>
           Power Rangers
          </i>
          related media ever, but here we are! And you know what? They own their roles so hard.
          <br/>
         </p>
         <p>
          I was picking up some serious
          <i>
           <a href="http://moviepilot.com/tags/halo--559681">
            Halo
           </a>
          </i>
          vibes throughout the whole thing, with a dash of tonal elements from
          <i>
           Blade Runner
          </i>
          and
          <i>
           Cloverfield
          </i>
          , along with definite shades of
          <i>
           The Raid
          </i>
          with those hyper-violent fight sequences. Seriously, the choreography and action in this short film was pretty damn good.
          <br/>
         </p>
         <figure data-id="275620">
          <img alt="Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?" itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_255,w_640/t_mp_quality/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-786a166a-7780-43a0-8026-634c7d536d42-png-275620.jpg" title="Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?"/>
          <figcaption>
           Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          I had never imagined
          <i>
           Power Rangers
          </i>
          the way Shankar/Kahn have here. That atmosphere and tone... it's bleak, it's sexy, it's moody, and weirdly enough it all somehow works. This clashing of genres seems to gel so well as an intense and epic sci-fi action thriller; who would have thought?
         </p>
         <p>
          As for my personal favorite bit from this short? The quick glimpses we got of Tommy Oliver suited up in his Ranger armor were pretty great. Why? Take a closer look at his Dragon Shield:
         </p>
         <figure data-id="275683">
          <img alt="Go, Green Ranger!" itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_256,w_640/t_mp_quality/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-green-ranger-png-275683.jpg" title="Go, Green Ranger!"/>
          <figcaption>
           Go, Green Ranger!
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Here it is in motion:
         </p>
         <figure data-id="275767">
          <video autoplay="autoplay" loop="loop" muted="muted" poster="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.jpg">
           <source src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.mp4" type="video/mp4">
           </source>
           <source src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.webm" type="video/webm">
           </source>
           <div class="mx-gif" data-pause_src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.jpg" data-play_src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.gif">
            <img src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.jpg"/>
            <i class="icon-play">
            </i>
            <div class="m-spinner">
             <i class="icon-spin">
             </i>
            </div>
           </div>
          </video>
          <figcaption>
           Go! Go! Go!
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          It's energy based! How cool is that. The nerd in me is geeking out so hard right now and the nostalgia hit me real good. I hope someone takes notice because I really need this to become a series. Maybe Netflix should pick this concept up, yeah? Not likely, but oh we can dream.
          <br/>
         </p>
         <h3>
          Will Lionsgate's
          <i>
           Power Rangers
          </i>
          reboot be as cool or slick as this short film? No way. It might be good, but if it's not, I'll at least have this short film to watch again. And again. And again.
         </h3>
         <div class="p-a-poll" data-poll="2725805">
          <div class="b-poll" data-prerendered="poll-2725805">

            <div class="b-p-question_wrapper">

             </a>

R-Rated Power Rangers Short Film is Violent, Bloody, and Straight Up BADASS!","html_body":"&lt;h3&gt;Lionsgate had better be worried about their upcoming &lt;i&gt;Power Rangers&lt;/i&gt; movie.&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;figure data-id=\"275736\"&gt;  &lt;img src=\"http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_191,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-7f3aba8a-8836-4bbb-8913-2306a4a3eaba-gif-275736.gif\" alt=\"\" title=\"\"&gt;  &lt;figcaption&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Why? Because film producer Adi Shankarthe man responsible for such awesome comic book related shorts as &lt;i&gt;&lt;a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7YDYL6oECjU\"&gt;Venom: Truth in Journalism&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt; and &lt;i&gt;&lt;a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bWpK0wsnitc\"&gt;The Punisher: Dirty Laundry&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt;just slapped the internet across the face with a big bag full of awesome bricks in the form of a &lt;i&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://moviepilot.com/tags/power-rangers\"&gt;Power Rangers&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt; short film put together by renowned music video director Joseph Kahn.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;This gritty take on a beloved franchise kicks so much ass, and it's righteously nuts. *NSFW* Prepare to have your mind blown:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;iframe class=\"embedly-embed\" src=\"//cdn.embedly.com/widgets/media.html?src=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fembed%2Fvw5vcUPyL90%3Ffeature%3Doembed&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3Dvw5vcUPyL90&amp;image=http%3A%2F%2Fi.ytimg.com%2Fvi%2Fvw5vcUPyL90%2Fhqdefault.jpg&amp;key=4346f5e0fac645ec8a30f75e92dc526f&amp;type=text%2Fhtml&amp;schema=youtube\" width=\"650\" height=\"366\" scrolling=\"no\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Sci-fi veteran Katee Sackhoff (&lt;i&gt;Battlestar Galactica, Riddick&lt;/i&gt;) as The Pink Ranger/Kimberly? Pretty awesome. James Van Der Beek (&lt;i&gt;Dawson's Creek&lt;/i&gt;) hamming it up as the primary antagonist and ex-Red Ranger Rocky? Also awesome. These are two actors with fairly decent fanbases who I would never have expected to show up in any kind of &lt;i&gt;Power Rangers&lt;/i&gt; related media ever, but here we are! And you know what? They own their roles so hard.&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;I was picking up some serious &lt;i&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://moviepilot.com/tags/halo--559681\"&gt;Halo&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt; vibes throughout the whole thing, with a dash of tonal elements from &lt;i&gt;Blade Runner &lt;/i&gt;and&lt;i&gt; Cloverfield&lt;/i&gt;, along with definite shades of &lt;i&gt;The Raid&lt;/i&gt; with those hyper-violent fight sequences. Seriously, the choreography and action in this short film was pretty damn good.&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;figure data-id=\"275620\"&gt;  &lt;img src=\"http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_511,w_1281/t_mp_quality/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-786a166a-7780-43a0-8026-634c7d536d42-png-275620.png\" alt=\"Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?\" title=\"Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?\"&gt;  &lt;figcaption&gt;Would you watch Katee Sackhoff in an R-Rated Power Rangers miniseries?&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;I had never imagined &lt;i&gt;Power Rangers&lt;/i&gt; the way Shankar/Kahn have here. That atmosphere and tone... it's bleak, it's sexy, it's moody, and weirdly enough it all somehow works. This clashing of genres seems to gel so well as an intense and epic sci-fi action thriller; who would have thought? &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;As for my personal favorite bit from this short? The quick glimpses we got of Tommy Oliver suited up in his Ranger armor were pretty great. Why? Take a closer look at his Dragon Shield: &lt;/p&gt;&lt;figure data-id=\"275683\"&gt;  &lt;img src=\"http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_513,w_1281/t_mp_quality/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-green-ranger-png-275683.png\" alt=\"Go, Green Ranger!\" title=\"Go, Green Ranger!\"&gt;  &lt;figcaption&gt;Go, Green Ranger!&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Here it is in motion:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;figure data-id=\"275767\"&gt;  &lt;img src=\"http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/image/upload/c_fill,h_192,w_480/t_mp_quality_gif/this-r-rated-power-rangers-short-film-is-violent-bloody-and-straight-up-badass-go-go-go-gif-275767.gif\" alt=\"Go! Go! Go!\" title=\"Go! Go! Go!\"&gt;  &lt;figcaption&gt;Go! Go! Go!&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;It's energy based! How cool is that. The nerd in me is geeking out so hard right now and the nostalgia hit me real good. I hope someone takes notice because I really need this to become a series. Maybe Netflix should pick this concept up, yeah? Not likely, but oh we can dream.&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;Will Lionsgate's &lt;i&gt;Power Rangers&lt;/i&gt; reboot be as cool or slick as this short film? No way. It might be good, but if it's not, I'll at least have this short film to watch again. And again.
